{"kind": "blogger#postList", "nextPageToken": "CgkIChjA2768yiUQy4Ca9ZL8nrwx", "items": [{"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "8003628325166672910", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-12-05T10:45:00+05:30", "updated": "2010-12-14T15:26:19+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMjkyMzIwNTc5NDYwCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/12/certificate-of-fitness-on-chemical.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/8003628325166672910", "title": "CERTIFICATE OF FITNESS ON CHEMICAL TANKERS --  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsfwGtgk6I/AAAAAAAABYs/rJDeSkGiPNk/s1600/download.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsfwGtgk6I/AAAAAAAABYs/rJDeSkGiPNk/s1600/download.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">&nbsp;<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: large;\">COF AND TRIPARTITE AGREEMENTS: &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: large;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><o:p></o:p><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">An In</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">ternational Certificate of Fitness for the Carriage of Dangerous Chemicals in Bulk shall be issued after an initial or renewal survey to a chemical tanker engaged in international voyages which complies with the relevant provisions of the Code.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Classification society issues the certificate of fitness on behalf of the administration.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">An International Certificate of Fitness for the Carriage of Dangerous Chemicals in Bulk shall be issued for a period specified by the Administration which shall not exceed 5 years.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"CM30\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">All ships will get a new COF after 1.1.07, considering IBC code and Marpol rules are revised as on 1.1.07. &nbsp;IMO has decided that Chemical carriers can carry COF or NLS, not&nbsp; both.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM30\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Ships with COF can carry IBC code chapter 17&nbsp; XYZ cargoes also-----&nbsp; while NLS certificated ships an carry IBC code Chapter 18, Category Z and&nbsp; OS cargoes only.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">For ships carrying IBC code chapter \u201c Other Substances\u201d OS, there is no need for COF, they require only NLS certificate.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><o:p><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">COF is a certificate issued by Flag administration confirming that the structure , equipment and materials used in the construction of the chemical tanker are in compliance to carry a given list of chemicals and it gives the conditions of carriage.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Upon receipt of cargo loading instructions, all products are to be checked against the Certificate of Fitness. Any irregularities are to be reported immediately to the chemical operator .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">However it must be understood that this by itself is not enough. The tank lining resistance tables must be consulted and only if both agree can the chemical be considered to be loaded. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM30\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Since new chemicals are being manufactured and re-evaluated for safe sea carriage regularly it may be possible that some chemical is not included in the COF list. In such a case permission may be obtained from flag administration or their representative for this particular chemical and attached to the COF as an addendum.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"CM30\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"CM30\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">The issuance of an Addendum to CoF may be done immediately based on the Tripartite Agreement. The submission of data and evaluation by GESAMP and ESPH may come afterwards. <o:p></o:p></span></div><h1 style=\"text-align: justify;\"><i><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: x-large;\">Tripartite Lists</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: small;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></i></h1><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"CM31\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">When there is a need to transport a bulk liquid cargo that has not been classified, the shippers have to go to their administration and request that a tripartite agreement be established between the shipping country, the receiving country, and the ship's flag state.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"CM31\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"CM31\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">That administration would need to receive the BLG Product Data Form. This is in accordance with Regulation 3(4) of MARPOL Annex II. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM31\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Because new products are continually being created and proposed for carriage onboard chemical tankers a mechanism ( Tripartite agreement ) has been created to provisionally classify these cargoes under the IMO guidelines.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">All non-ANNEX 1 cargoes carried in bulk are classified by the International Maritime Organization (IMO) and/or the vessel's flag state. The carriage requirements for a product are then determined by these entities using the guidelines set out by GESAMP and the IMO<span lang=\"EN-GB\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Conditions of carriage of chemicals not included in COF are the subject of a \u201ctripartite agreement \u201cinvolving flag state and port administrations and included in the addendum. It is an agreement between 3 parties.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Products that are not shown in Chapter 17 and 18 of the IBC Code.&nbsp; Invariably such products have been subject to a provisional categorisation and are identified as potential entries to the IBC Code in the IMO Tripartite Agreement Lists.&nbsp; <span style=\"color: black;\">Tripartite agreements are valid for three years. It is an agreement between :-</span> the port state of the shipper, the flag state of the carrier and the port state receiving the cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">If a tripartite agreement is completed it is then included in the \"Provisional Categorization of Liquid Substances\" (also known as the MEPC.2 Circular).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"CM31\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">An updated circular is published every December. The initiator of the tripartite agreement has three years in which to provide all of the required data to formally classify a substance. It is not acceptable to repeatedly initiate new tripartite agreements for the same product. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM31\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"CM31\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">&nbsp;The 2005 version of MEPC.2/Circ. (Tripartite Lists), to be issued on 17 December this year, will feature two versions of List 1, one valid until 31 December 2006 and one valid from 01 January 2007 onwards. Cargoes missing from IBC code would appear in the MEPC.2/Circ. until such time as the next amendment to the IBC Code is undertaken (probably 2009).</span> <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM31\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div class=\"CM26\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">The tripartite agreement will stand for three years, before which time all outstanding or otherwise necessary data will have to have been forwarded to the IMO (GESAMP) for the formal classification. Otherwise the tripartite agreement will expire. If the cargo is assessed as being regulated by the IBC Code or MARPOL Annex II, the ship's Certificate of Fitness and Procedures &amp; Arrangements Manual will have to be amended (usually by the classification society, arranged by the owner or manager).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM26\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"CM26\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">&nbsp;The shipping country will determine the provisional carriage requirements per Annex I of MEPC/Circ.265, and seek the concurrence of the flag state and receiving countries using the standard fax format per Annex 7 of MEPC/Circ.265. The IMO and other involved administrations should also be copied.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"CM26\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"CM26\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">&nbsp;In the absence of a response from the flag state or receiving countries after 14 days, the agreement may be deemed to have been accepted, and the IMO is informed. If there is a question as to whether the cargo has been classified, the International Bulk Chemical Code (IBC Code) should be consulted. If not found there, check the annual \"Provisional Categorization of Liquid Substances\", the most recent of which is MEPC.2/Circ11. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">P&amp;A manual contains info on MP, viscocity, water solubility and ventable cargoes .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc_PWG1M4I/AAAAAAAAB58/lY1XTxvbORk/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc_PWG1M4I/AAAAAAAAB58/lY1XTxvbORk/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\">-------CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )<o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><br />\n</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "13", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/8003628325166672910/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "3467434589310365838", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-12-05T10:23:00+05:30", "updated": "2018-06-27T06:01:30+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNTMwMDU5NDkwNzUzCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/12/on-trail-of-truth-capt-ajit-vadakayil.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/3467434589310365838", "title": "ON THE TRAIL OF TRUTH --   CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRV9nHcv-VI/AAAAAAAACU4/2dn9wPQ7hiE/s1600/dark.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"200\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRV9nHcv-VI/AAAAAAAACU4/2dn9wPQ7hiE/s1600/dark.JPG\" width=\"185\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: x-large;\"><b><span style=\"background-color: cyan;\">Ancient Indian &nbsp;</span><span style=\"color: red;\">- Metaphysics&nbsp;</span>, &nbsp; <span style=\"color: blue;\">Dielectics&nbsp;</span>, &nbsp; <span style=\"color: purple;\">Epistemology , &nbsp;</span><span style=\"color: magenta;\">Empiricism</span></b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsTR3RepHI/AAAAAAAABWw/yh6ki3-_R4Y/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsTR3RepHI/AAAAAAAABWw/yh6ki3-_R4Y/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" width=\"311\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A ship captains job ( who must be the jack of all trades ) offers plenty on a emotional , spiritual and mental level.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The human mind has inherent weaknesses. It can be raped at will by people who know how to do it.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsTMR37viI/AAAAAAAABWs/y9Sc4dr6c14/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"200\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsTMR37viI/AAAAAAAABWs/y9Sc4dr6c14/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" width=\"131\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A quarter century ago, I had walked into a captains cabin to take over command of the ship. &nbsp;The outgoing master was in animated conference with the bosun and the ships laundryman. &nbsp;From the laundryman\u2019s \u201c I don\u2019t give a damn \u201c , body language I could see that he that he was on the warpath.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Both sailors were sent away and we settled down to the formal process of handing / taking over command. I could see that the outgoing captain could not harness his mind to the job\u2014his mind was chattering . So I asked him, what transpired with the laundryman.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">To cut a long story short, the laundryman had refused to do a particular job. He was right, and he had a point. For he was employed to wash stewards uniforms ( white tunics and pants ) \u2013 not civilian clothes. At the same time the stewards had a point, as they had won civilian clothes on duty due to water rationing at a long anchorage.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I told the captain \u201c you just call him back and I will make him agree to what he refused to do , just a few minutes ago\u2014 even if he was sacked or his knee caps were broken\u201d.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I then took a A4 size paper and wrote down 10 questions , whose answers required the answer YES.&nbsp; The last and 10<sup>th</sup> question would be \u201c are you willing to wash the clothes , you refused to wash\u201d . <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The captain was clean bowled. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Here was a guy telling that he could do the impossible. He wanted to see the questionnaire , and I gave it to him. All I wanted him to do was sit in the bedroom behind the curtains and hear the proceedings\u2014to check if I followed the script.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">So pretty soon the bosun and laundryman were called back.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I shot off the first question, after introducing myself as the new captain.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; A cloud appears to consist of some white, fleecy substance, although in reality it is a concentration of drops of water.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPscPHLN_5I/AAAAAAAABYY/m_tHsu3K9iY/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPscPHLN_5I/AAAAAAAABYY/m_tHsu3K9iY/s1600/images.jpg\" width=\"398\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"></span>It is the<b> </b>study and science of first principles or ultimate irrefutable truths. the two descriptions of the subject would thus be two sides of a single coin.. it. Scientific theories can be brought to the test of experience, whereas metaphysical theories cannot.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Metaphysician is a sort of super scientist, unlimited in his curiosity and gifted with a capacity for putting together other people's findings with a skill and imagination that none of them individually commands. &nbsp;He can refute by debate, through a method for systematic evaluation of definitions.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Quantum physics , is a branch of physics providing a mathematical description of much of the dual particle-like and wave-like behavior and interactions of energy and matter. It departs from classical mechanics primarily at the atomic and subatomic scales, the so-called quantum realm.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In advanced topics of quantum mechanics, some of these behaviors are macroscopic and only emerge at very low or very high energies or temperatures.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsWt-qGQMI/AAAAAAAABXk/nGt7J_6q2gs/s1600/images+%252814%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: purple;\"><span class=\"inlinetitle\"><b><span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-size: large;\">Dialectic</span></b></span>,</span> in philosophy, method of investigating the nature of truth by the criticism of initial concepts and hypotheses. &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The ancient Indian Vedic d<span class=\"inlinetitle\" style=\"color: black;\">ialectic is based on a dialogue between two or more people who may hold differing views, yet wish to pursue truth by seeking agreement with one another.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"inlinetitle\" style=\"color: black;\"><br /></span></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"inlinetitle\"><br /></span></span></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsc9YAlPNI/AAAAAAAABYk/XJeu4xLlB6E/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"333\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsc9YAlPNI/AAAAAAAABYk/XJeu4xLlB6E/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"inlinetitle\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"inlinetitle\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This is in contrast to debate, in which two or more people hold differing views and wish to persuade or prove one another wrong (and thus a jury or judge is needed to decide the matter), or rhetoric, which is a relatively long oration conducted by a single person.<o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"inlinetitle\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsd4VXMwjI/AAAAAAAABYo/-UUiFVqdGfU/s1600/images+%25289%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">Pythogarus ( 570 BC \u2013\n495 BC ),&nbsp; Heraclitus ( 535 BC-- 475\nBC),&nbsp; Socrates ( 469 BC- 399 BC ) and\nPlato (427 BC to 347 BC ) studied in Kerala, India .&nbsp;&nbsp; One of the much hyped up western thinkers German\nGeorg Wilhelm Friedrich Hegel (1770 -1831 AD) &nbsp;lifted from ancient Indian concepts without\nany understanding of the spiritual thought procedures.</span></b><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"inlinetitle\"><b><span style=\"background-color: yellow; color: black; font-size: large;\">Empiricism</span></b></span><span style=\"color: black;\">, is&nbsp; a doctrine that affirms that all ideas and knowledge are a posteriori, that is, derived from and based on experience, and denies that they can ever be a priori, that is, discoverable without having to rely on the senses.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsVNyDWIII/AAAAAAAABXU/MY-Rr_d4aKc/s1600/download.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsVNyDWIII/AAAAAAAABXU/MY-Rr_d4aKc/s1600/download.JPG\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Laws that express&nbsp; relationships between phenomena, without making any claims about the underlying causes of the phenomena, are called empirical laws.&nbsp; The meaning of the term experience is generally limited to the impressions and sensations received by the senses.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Thus, knowledge is the information apprehended by the five sense modalities\u2014 hearing, seeing, touching, tasting, and smelling. Such knowledge is always about matters of fact, about what one can see, touch, hear, taste, or smell.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsVLO2BgzI/AAAAAAAABXQ/kwvV5v3ke0w/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsVLO2BgzI/AAAAAAAABXQ/kwvV5v3ke0w/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" width=\"261\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">For strict empiricists this definition has the implication that the human mind is passive\u2014it is an organ that receives impressions and more or less records them as they are. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Empiricism then, in the philosophy of science, emphasizes those aspects of scientific knowledge that are closely related to evidence, especially as discovered in experiments.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is a fundamental part of the scientific method that all hypotheses and theories must be tested against observations of the natural world, rather than resting solely on a priori reasoning, intuition, or revelation. Hence, science is considered to be methodologically empirical in nature.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsVx4jrU2I/AAAAAAAABXY/W1UB4EgDmMY/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsVx4jrU2I/AAAAAAAABXY/W1UB4EgDmMY/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Pseudophone, an instrument made of two ear trumpets, one leading from the right side of the head to the left ear and the other vice versa. This created the illusory impression of reversed localization of sound. While walking along the street wearing the pseudophone he would hear footsteps to his right when they actually came from the left. If you put this on your pet cat\u2014it upsets its natural instincts.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsXFygcL3I/AAAAAAAABXs/0uJwKkXK0Nw/s1600/images+%252816%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsXFygcL3I/AAAAAAAABXs/0uJwKkXK0Nw/s1600/images+%252816%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<h6>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: small; font-weight: normal;\">Rainbows result from refraction.<a href=\"ebcid:com.britannica.oec2.identifier.IndexEntryContentIdentifier?idxStructId=163008&amp;library=EB\"></a><a href=\"ebcid:com.britannica.oec2.identifier.ArticleIdentifier?articleId=30419&amp;library=STANDARD&amp;query=null&amp;title=#9030419.toc\"></a>&nbsp;Mirage&nbsp;, the vision of a pool of water is created by light passing the layers of hot air above the heated surface of a highway.&nbsp; Under unusual conditions, more elaborate mirages appear as UFOs'.<o:p></o:p></span></h6>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsXTRakB3I/AAAAAAAABXw/M93bl8JhyKE/s1600/images+%252817%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsXTRakB3I/AAAAAAAABXw/M93bl8JhyKE/s1600/images+%252817%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<h6>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: small; font-weight: normal;\">Sudden temperature&nbsp;contrasts can play tricks on the senses. If hot water is run over one hand, and cold water over the other long enough for both to adjust to the temperatures and both are then plunged into lukewarm water, the resulting sensation will be that the cold hand will feel warm and the hot, cold.&nbsp;</span></h6>\n<h6>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: small; font-weight: normal;\">It would seem that in plunging the cold-adapted hand, nerve cells for perceiving cold were suddenly inhibited and those for perceiving hot were suddenly stimulated, while in the hot-adapted hand the reverse took place.</span></h6>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsX7LKWDvI/AAAAAAAABX0/HA2IFpPX06w/s1600/images+%252818%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsX7LKWDvI/AAAAAAAABX0/HA2IFpPX06w/s1600/images+%252818%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In most Indian movie halls they put AC at high setting when you enter and when you are about to leave. This gives the impression that the cinema runs good AC and value for your money. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">Smell</span><span style=\"color: black;\"><b>&nbsp;</b></span><span style=\"color: black;\">(olfactory) discrimination is influenced by any odour to which the olfactory structures already have adapted. Receptors&nbsp;in the nose, however, adapt quickly and cease to respond to a particular stimulus producing so-called olfactory fatigue.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><br /></span></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">Thus, an odour that is strong at first will gradually become imperceptible, as happens when one becomes unaware of the smell of his own BO. There may also be present the phenomenon of masking,&nbsp;&nbsp;this is a decrease in sensitivity to one odour after exposure to another (for example, a strong-smelling disinfectant).</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When you go to a perfume shop\u2014before you make a final choice and &nbsp;buy a perfume, reset your olfactory senses by smelling on coffee beans . Or you may well be buying a bad overpriced perfume. The perfume saleswomen , who get private commissions , are good in getting rid of such stuff to naive customers.<br clear=\"all\" style=\"mso-special-character: line-break;\" /> <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsYPtA2KSI/AAAAAAAABX4/SlPQKAYkdCk/s1600/images+%252820%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsYPtA2KSI/AAAAAAAABX4/SlPQKAYkdCk/s1600/images+%252820%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The human ear&nbsp;typically serves to distinguish between about 1,500 levels of pitch. Are you not able to ping the voice on the other side of the phone?.&nbsp; &nbsp;The number of discriminable tones is in the hundred thousands.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When two sounds are heard in close succession (time error once more) the intensity or loudness of the second is judged by comparing it with the first, and is relative. Thus, a murmur may sound loud when compared to a whisper, or a \u201cdeafening\u201d noise may make all other sounds inaudible.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsYoumIh9I/AAAAAAAABX8/ozpUbGNz7-0/s1600/images+%252821%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsYoumIh9I/AAAAAAAABX8/ozpUbGNz7-0/s1600/images+%252821%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The hum of an electric fan may help to diffuse the street noises of traffic and thus improve the discrimination of TV sounds in the room. Folks living at busy streets , unable to study , sleep or watch TV must try this out.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Synesthesia may be induced with drugs, Hearing, sight, smell, taste, and touch are regarded as the classical five senses. Touch has a multiplicity of subdivisions, including the senses of pressure, heat, cold, and pain. Scientists have determined the existence of as many as 15 additional senses.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Sense organs buried deep in the tissues of muscles, tendons, and joints, for example, give rise to sensations of weight, position of the body, and amount of bending of the various joints; these organs are called proprioceptors. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsY3Cxn6oI/AAAAAAAABYA/CRbmcNWNwEI/s1600/images+%252822%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"200\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsY3Cxn6oI/AAAAAAAABYA/CRbmcNWNwEI/s1600/images+%252822%2529.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Within the semicircular canal of the ear is the organ of equilibrium, concerned with the sense of balance. General senses, which produce information concerning bodily needs (hunger, thirst, fatigue, and pain), are also recognized.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsZOlqCIaI/AAAAAAAABYE/icbd8RJ-iX8/s1600/images+%252823%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsZOlqCIaI/AAAAAAAABYE/icbd8RJ-iX8/s1600/images+%252823%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Stimulation through one sense may enhance the function of another. Seeing a merry go round&nbsp; may activate the sense of balance in an observer to the point at which it causes seasickness.&nbsp; A picture of appetizing food may evoke sensations of taste and smell.</span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;( ever notice this?&nbsp; when you see shit, biological reflex is to salivate, social reflex is to spit. )<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The surgeon general has ordered that repulsive mouth cancer pictures must be printed on cigarette packs to discourage your from smoking.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsZZUVUyyI/AAAAAAAABYI/Z9MsETFOK4E/s1600/images+%252824%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsZZUVUyyI/AAAAAAAABYI/Z9MsETFOK4E/s1600/images+%252824%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Sensory rivalry, is when one stimulus inhibits the perception of another.. In a similar way, some dentists use auditory analgesia (a \u201cmasking\u201d of pain by sound)&nbsp; . Most Tatoo parlours use music to mask the pain.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"artcopy1\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Emotions&nbsp;or strong expectations frequently cause illusional misperceptions in everyday life. The hostile listener hears someone say \u201cwire\u201d and thinks he is being called a \u201cliar\u201d; The self-consciously obese girl misinterprets the word \u201cfate\u201d as \u201cweight.\u201d </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsanFJ-cNI/AAAAAAAABYU/byEM2M8GxDc/s1600/images+%252825%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"357\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPsanFJ-cNI/AAAAAAAABYU/byEM2M8GxDc/s1600/images+%252825%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<b><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<b><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; IT CAN BE EVALUATED BY A SIMPLE COMPUTER..<br /><br /><span style=\"color: red; font-size: 16px;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/12/marine-engineering-self-examiner-ships.html</span><br /><br />WHEN YOU GO FOR A DRIVING TEST IN INDIA--YOU FIRST HAVE TO CLEAR THIS TYPE OF OBJECTIVE EXAM..<br /><br /><b><span style=\"color: magenta; font-size: medium;\">A HALF WIT CAN PASS AN OBJECTIVE EXAM..</span></b><br /><br />THEN WHAT IS A SUBJECTIVE EVALUATION?<br /><br />IT IS BUILDING AN IDEA FROM SCRATCH LIKE AN ESSAY .. font-size: 16pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>SULPHURIC ACID<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-jDO7Rt68Oxs/TjdbLRLaL6I/AAAAAAAAE8c/LZfuJhToDIA/s1600/P3180099.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-jDO7Rt68Oxs/TjdbLRLaL6I/AAAAAAAAE8c/LZfuJhToDIA/s320/P3180099.jpg\" width=\"228\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sulphuric acid is a rogue cargo and many seamen have been injured badly.</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><br />\n</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">It is the free flowing high density property that makes the cargo dangerous especially on the maiden trip with Teflon gaskets being inserted not bolted. <o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><br />\n</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">The only time Chemical carriage becomes more dangerous is when you discharge highly toxic , high MP cargoes like Phenol or HMD in freezing weather.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Imagine a slug of free flowing Sulphuric acid being projected through a pipe by compressed air of 7 kg which you deliberately introduce into the pipelines at stripping time. It will smash into all corners like a bullet. Stripping the stack is hence a dangerous job ( especially on the maiden voyage ) and the person doing it must wear proper PPE. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">IT TENDS TO GET INTO THE HYDRAULIC SYSTEM OF JAPANESE DEEPWELL PUMPS. The Frank Mohn system has a jockey pump which keeps 2 kg pressure in the system at all times\u2014this is something which the Japanese pumps do not have. They are solely dependant on the air buffer inside the cofferdam which can leak out slowly as air tends to find the highest point. Also it is difficult to find out if the air pressure has reduced\u2014as there is no pressure guage.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Since Sulphuric acid is highly reactive with water causing exhothermic reaction when water to added to acid , it follows that the double skin must not have any water. This is an item the port state inspector can check.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Properties:<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Colourless or clear brown depending on purity.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Dense oily liquid <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Normally carried at concentration &gt;90% at temp &lt; 35C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">CHRIS / SFA<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Marpol cat/ Y<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">UN number/ 1830<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Fosfa approved<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">MP/ 10.4C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Surface tension/ high<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">SG/ 1.84<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">AH/ 30C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sulphuric acid is Non-flammable<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Has no odour but when hot the odour is choking.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">It is a good last cargo for WWT<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Completely water soluble.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sulfuric acid will not bum. It will react with many metals, giving off hydrogen gas that is highly flammable. If hydrogen is trapped in a confined space, it can form an explosive mixture with air.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Do not use water to put out fire if the water can get into concentrated Sulfuric acid. Use respiratory protection against fumes.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">May cause moderate irritating, unpleasant at high concentrations<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Severe skin irritant, causing second and third-degree bums on short contact and very injurious to the eyes<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Some hazard, typically having threshold limits of 100 to 500 ppm.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Odor threshold (ppm)<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Greater then 1 mg/m3<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Permissible exposure limits/TWA<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>1 mg/m3<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Liquid causes severe bums with destruction of tissue. Vapor is very irritating.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The inhalation hazard is slight at ordinary temperatures. The skin on which acid is spilled may feel hot or it may sting or itch. Drench<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>with<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>water.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Skin<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>contact:<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>remove contaminated clothing and flush affected areas gently with large amounts of water.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Eye contact: immediately flush eyes gently with water, continue to flush for 15 minutes. Get medical attention.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Stable, but can react very easily with many other materials.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Highly corrosive to most metals, particularly at concentrations below 60 %. May cause wood or cellulose to ignite.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">USCG/ Group 2. See also exceptions to the chart<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Wear rubber gloves, protective clothing. Have body shield available. Avoid contact with liquid. If there is a leak on cargo transfer system, stop the transfer and empty the line system. Secure ignition sources. Flush contaminated area with large amounts of water.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">MARPOL Pollution category<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>/ Y<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">SPECIAL ARRANGEMENTS<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Have on board sufficient acid resistant hoses , Polypropelene or SS for the cargo transfer.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Have on board sufficient SS acid spray shields to cover flanges on manifold and hose connections according to IBC code.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">PRELOADING PRECAUTIONS<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sulfuric Acid is normally carried in stainless steel tanks with a minimum concentration of 90% and at temperatures not exceeding 35C.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">PREPARATIONS FOR LOADING<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The tank must be cleaned to<b> </b><span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">\"Visual Water White Standard\",</span> and free of any residues from previous cargoes, chlorides and any other foreign matters.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">It is a good idea to passivate the tanks with 14% cold nitric acid to build up the passive layer of Chromium oxide which can get denuded by hot salt water wash.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Heating coils to be pressure-tested for leaks, blown empty and dried with nitrogen. The tank must be dry before loading is permitted.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The surrounding cofferdams and double bottoms must be empty and dry.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">DISCHARGING</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Because of the high gravity of Sulfuric Acid, very high pump pressure may be experienced. In such cases care must be taken not to quickly open or close valves in the pump system as this causes pressure surges that may rupture lines or hoses.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">CLEANING<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\"> PRECAUTION</span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sulfuric Acid in less than 30-70% concentrations is non-oxidizing and attacks the steel rapidly, particularly at elevated temperatures.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">When concentrated Sulfuric Acid is diluted the reaction is exothermic and the temperature of acid will rapidly increase. If the tank is cleaned with inadequate quantities of water, the acid will become hot, as it is diluted, and rapid attack will occur on the stainless steel until sufficient water is introduced. Large quantities (preferably fresh water) must be put into the tank to rapidly pass the dangerous concentration range and heat increase. Preferably if stainless steel hoses were used on the manifold for discharge should be replaced with non-stainless steel acid resistant hose(es) before the cleaning operation starts.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">CLEANING</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Preferably, fresh water should be used as cleaning medium but if not available large amounts of sea water must be used/added to the tank. Cleaning must start as soon as possible after discharge, but do not commence cleaning unless slop disposal is available, either to shore or as per Marpol regulations.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sulfuric Acid slops should normally not be kept on board as diluted acid slops arc very aggressive to all metals. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Cleaning with water (adding water to acid) will generate much heat with release of Hydrogen gas.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Cleaning must be started with as much water as possible introduced into the tank from the beginning. If it is not possible to pump washings overboard after water quenching , leave the tank alone. Close all inlets to prevent moisture ingress into tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Continuously drain the tank, do not allow acid/water mixture to collect in the tank.<b> Do not stop cleaning before the pH check reads 7.</b><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If seawater was used, the tank must be immediately desalted with freshwater.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ensure that the line systems, including the vent system, are cleaned out and free of any acid remains.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Flush out the heating coils with freshwater and check for acidity using pH paper.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">When diluted to 50% Sulphuric acid becomes the most corrosive. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Don\u2019t EVER retain slops on board.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sulphuric acid is hygroscopic. When you load slack tanks due to the load density\u2014bear this in mind.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><i>Sulphuric acid has the tendency to eat away the under water Annex 2 pipeline, on the section below the water level to the overboard &nbsp;.</i></span><br />\n<br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;
