margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nhere is my piece on ON BOARD MENTORING.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nwhat is mentoring?</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nit is an inexpensive way to build up a high performance team on board , like a formula one ferrari team. HIGH PERFORMANCE TEAMS DO NOT HAPPEN--THEY ARE BUILT.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\ndifference between OBT and OBM:</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nthe mentor retains a STRANGE CONTROL over the trainee even after the session is over. for the trainer treats the mind as a vessel to be filled up, while the mentor treats it as a STACK TO BE IGNITED. sceptics pl consider-- capt vadakayil had mentored capt ajay prasad. does any body feel that he would not have joined selandia/ fairchem colt as per my wishes because he would get two thousand dollars more elsewhere. or capt sanjay mehta whom i had mentored will not jump from copenhagen pool to singapore pool when ever i want him to? in short the obt informs,--the obm INFLUENCES and MOTIVATES.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nneed for interaction:--</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nany idiot can evaluate knowledge by a written test. evaluating attitudes need personal interaction. ATTITUDES are beliefs and values. they are more sophisticated than skills and not easily influenced by a mere trainer.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nexample of a mentor:</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nthe full bird colonel of rambo who keeps mouthing glib patronising talk like \" what are friends for?\".&nbsp;</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPisr_bWIeI/AAAAAAAABSE/40rRN2L-O3s/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPisr_bWIeI/AAAAAAAABSE/40rRN2L-O3s/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nit is a skill in itself. 'glib patronising talk' usually created resentment if the student is intelligent. the mentors personality is such that he gets the team excited about waht they NEED to learn rather than what they WANT to learn. he does not fight fire with fire.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nqualifications of a mentor:</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nhe must be SEASONED, COMPASSIONATE , FAIR and have character --only then he can be a role model. HIS STYLE MUST NOT BE DOMINATING (that is why the master is a misfit , he can aleniate the trainee who feels threatened ) but facilitating. there is no need to catch a cat by the tail in order to know more about it---unless the cat is real bad (tee hee ! ) since feedback is the fuel for improved performance, the mentor must be honest only to the extent that his feedback cannot be destructive. negative feed back without splitting hairs ,must not be untimely and unbalanced. negative feedback cant be in public. the feedback game is like a game of billiards. let me not digress--</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nmoving on--</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nthe mentor MOULDS ATTITUDES and HONES COMMITMENT. an ordinary teacher can address only knowledge and skills. he cannot CHANGE BEHAVIOR like a mentor. greg chapell can be a good coach because he talks about mentoring. the team must delight in the self improvement process. unless it is meaningful fun doing all this , this process cannot work. he must get interested in the team and in the process the team gets interested in him. he will address crewmembers by their first names.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nwhy on board? why not in the institute?</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nlike the universal water the mentor must find the level of every member and float him up like how the panamax is floated up in the canal ( tee heee ! ). this is called PITCHING AT THE RIGHT LEVEL. the mentoring ENVIRONMENT is important. executive ship management has build a stainless steel tank with a framo pump inside in their training institute spending a fortune.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nenvironment--</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nif the environment is not ok , the dialogue between minds cannot happen. remember the mentor does not bid you to enter the glorious house of his own wisdom--rather HE LEADS YOU TO THE THRESHOLD OF YOUR OWN MIND.(oops, have i been too profound about mind exploration?) the mentor is a PROBER NOT AN INTERROGATOR.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nwhy stacks?--</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nthe mentor must not waste too much on time on spent forces. my chief engineer on sichem psv was a spent force. i stop short of calling him a loser. wet stacks can be dried and ignited.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nfood for the soul--</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nthe obm must identify people who do not take pride in their work and encourage these misguided souls as long as they are not persistant story tellers who want company policy change to suit their needs.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nbottomline--</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nwhile getting off the ship the obm must have the satisfaction of knowing that he has bridged the gap between what the team wants to learn and what they need to know. he must have with him a list of the crew's future training needs . he cannot get off with a conflict left to fester which he has not attempted to diffuse. I WOULD CALL A MENTOR SUCCESSFUL ONLY IF HE HAS ESTABLISED A CULTURE WHICH ENCOURAGES A CREW MEMBER TO STAY WITH THE COMPANY AND FLOURISH. he has done a damn good job if he has identified people who have a sense on belonging. for what is the use in sharing insight and experience with such driftwood.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n#########</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nMENTORING--- VIEWED INSIDE OUT</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nLAST TIME I GAVE A BIRDS EYE VIEW OF THE POND OF MENTORING.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTHIS TIME I AM DIVING RIGHT IN.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n--HERE I GO!!---YIPEEEEE!!!!</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nMID AIR LET ME DIGRESS\u2014</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nPEOPLE WHO GOT MENTORED BY CAPT VADAKAYIL WILL CRY---\u201cHE NEVER PRACTISED A DANG WORD OF ALL THIS\u201d. I SHALL CONFIRM ---. YES THEY ARE RIGHT . I NEVER FOLLOWED A WORD OF ALL THIS FOR I DID \u201cSPONTANEOUS HUMOR MENTORING\u201d.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTHERE IS NO CRASH COURSE TO THIS ART. IF YOU ARE NOT BORN WITH THIS ART YOU MUST BE A LIVING LEGEND LIKE MARADONA TO IGNORE WHAT FOLLOWS.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDIGRESSION CODE TWO\u2014I WILL DELIBERATELY LEAVE MY PROSE DISJOINTED AND UNEDITED. THIS IS TO MAKE MY PIECE MORE POWERFUL.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nSCEPTICS PL CONSIDER---WOULD ARUNDATHI ROY HAVE GOT THE BOOKER PRIZE FOR HER NOVEL \u2018 GOD OF SMALL THINGS\u2019 IF SHE HAD NOT STREWN THE STORY AROUND IN BITS AND PIECES FOR THE READER TO WEAVE-- AFTER READING IT AT LEAST TWICE?</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nSplaaaaashhhh!!</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nFirst let me swim around and locate TRUTHS etched on rock. ---</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPitlonHq0I/AAAAAAAABSM/XB9AG2ZiEx0/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPitlonHq0I/AAAAAAAABSM/XB9AG2ZiEx0/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nHumor is a state of mind which can appreciate the ludicrous or absurdly incongruous. It instills a feeling of camaraderie. Human beings are by nature playful creatures. Leaders who are open to humor become more human and approachable. Only humor can save people who are on the brink of burnout.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nFrivolousness or behaving like Mr.Super Dick (or prick for the matter) is just not the humor I am referring to..</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPitvGp6xtI/AAAAAAAABSQ/2G2MG8Olf0o/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPitvGp6xtI/AAAAAAAABSQ/2G2MG8Olf0o/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nProductivity increases when commitment increases. Committed employees value their existing work relationship so highly that they may even pass over another job which pays 2000 usd more. Committed employees speak well about the company to the seafaring community. Only people who are happy in their work can be committed. A heightened atmosphere of general goodwill exists on such a ship..</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nWhen you trust people they trust you in return. When a high level of trust exists sailors show very little concern about getting their share from a relationship because they know for sure the other party will not take advantage of them. People in low trust relationships are preoccupied with seeing that they get their share of the relationship -- ( like high wages , new ships) and the other party gets no more than a fair share.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPit2RZcVAI/AAAAAAAABSU/5c0-8064vUo/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPit2RZcVAI/AAAAAAAABSU/5c0-8064vUo/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTrust is fragile and can be destroyed in one single stroke. Trust is not being gullible to believe bullshit or be treated like a mushroom ( always in the dark and fed with lot of crap).</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nFirst loyalty is to yourself\u2014this is the way human beings are made.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nEmployees have a right to be treated with courtesy and respect. Rewards have little meaning if respect is missing. ( I learnt this in Zodiac-- the only thing I learnt there other than sabbath) They have a right to expect the management to care about their happiness and safety.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nSailors are proud to be part of an organization that show ethical consideration for themselves and for society and even the environment (many superintendents develop a nelsons eye when they see the merlin pipe used to pump ho sludge overboard) . They get inspired to bond and commit to such an organisation.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nAlmost all new employees want to stay in an organization and do a good job.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nQuality is a culture which must be built in \u2013not inspected in semi annually.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiuBn39gaI/AAAAAAAABSY/4PklLJ7styk/s1600/images+%25289%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiuBn39gaI/AAAAAAAABSY/4PklLJ7styk/s1600/images+%25289%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTime is required to build skills necessary to meet quality standards. OBM cuts down this time.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTrust goes out of the window when you ask for ideas and don\u2019t follow up on them. All that is required is to comment on unfeasible ideas. Or the next time you ask for ideas they crew wont trust you enough to give you time of day.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nCommitment to a common goal is the foundation of success. Commitment and loyalty come from being included rather than excluded in decision making and information sharing (sometimes the crew does not know where the ship is bound for\u2014thus starting the galley news bureau with the captains steward as the news reader). Commitment to the company improves when employees are recogonised for their contributions.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiuMYUQdbI/AAAAAAAABSc/_U4C0pWMxrM/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiuMYUQdbI/AAAAAAAABSc/_U4C0pWMxrM/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nNegative attitudes are contagious.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nThe strongest drive in human nature is the desire to be appreciated.(don\u2019t take my word for granted and call an ugly girl, gorgeous, for she will haul you over burning embers for sexual harassment ). If it is overdone with insincerity it becomes patronizing.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nPatronisers compliment people to serve themselves and does not care for the dignity of others.. Loud praises of few people is bound to cause others to feel left out and will cause resentment.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiuVX6SlUI/AAAAAAAABSg/MAYT632eQvY/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiuVX6SlUI/AAAAAAAABSg/MAYT632eQvY/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nPraise seldom improves \u201cperformance\u201d rather in some cases it impairs performance. It may lead some duffers to believe that they are better than what they are. So instead of praise try giving them feed back which encourages them.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTwo of the most powerful motivators are survival and security. Criticism threatens motivation.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nCompany seminars must not be used to pit workers against management. When respectable top bosses are put in the witness box on the defensive\u2014even after the issues are settled , deep scars are left behind. Defensive blocking burns energy needed for constructive action.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nThe quickest way to destroy trust is to jump all over somebody who is doing his best.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTrust and delegation go hand in hand. This does not imply abdication or dumping\u2014for delegation is built on trust \u2013not abandonment.( or even micromanaging\u2014hovering over. I did that on Sichem Pearl for 2 months ).</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiu5SEpnNI/AAAAAAAABSo/7nmtXOqiKGs/s1600/images+%252812%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiu5SEpnNI/AAAAAAAABSo/7nmtXOqiKGs/s1600/images+%252812%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDeparting employees take a great deal of knowledge with them. Losing good employees has a domino effect.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiusOvw_GI/AAAAAAAABSk/4l27fKkp_Ao/s1600/download.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiusOvw_GI/AAAAAAAABSk/4l27fKkp_Ao/s1600/download.JPG\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nBurned out employees make huge mistakes ---the intelligent ones just simply quit. An unhappy ship leads to burnout. Vetting inspectors rarely punish a ship where the crew morale is high and ships management radiates pride.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nShips are run by men not machines.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nCreativity involves people talking together\u2014even at coffee breaks.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nJob satisfaction is a major factor for an employees decision to stay with or leave the company. High turnover makes it difficult to build a chemical pool.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nCommunicating well is is one of the lowest cost but highest yielding things that you can do to keep employee retention.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nWhere there is low commitment there exists a mentality of every man for himself.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nNow let me define VISION. It is always seen when in ecstasy. It is a deep optimistic expression of what is desired.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPivFODne5I/AAAAAAAABSs/xcfsp3JCL4w/s1600/images+%252813%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPivFODne5I/AAAAAAAABSs/xcfsp3JCL4w/s1600/images+%252813%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nWhat vision should a standard company like TESMA hold for the future.\u2014</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nLet me talk about the company ORGANISATION CHART.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nWhen I was at the Japanese shipyard at Usuki I got familiar with the pyramid structure. Fine\u2014but the pyramid base consisted of morons who made stupid mistakes. Another familiar structure is in the company manual consisting of many boxes.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIdeally the chart for the future should look like the anatomy of the nervous system of a human body. Sense organ messages from brain (or management) must be sent to only that part of the body (or employees) best suited to handle the job ( or change ). Individual talent and synergy of teamwork is utilized.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTHIS IS WHERE THE MENTORING ASPECT COMES IN. Mentoring helps build the network and skills for such a proactively responsive organization. Mentoring is here to stay and will be a way of life in the future.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTESMA Singapore can take the credit for being the pioneer and discoverer of the term OBM . Mentoring must not be limited to ships , but should be a culture ashore too. The company realizes that mentoring is not a luxury but a necessity.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nKnowledge and skills of every employee is harnessed to get the cutting edge. OBM will first be kick started on chemical tankers where know how has been scarce and hard to acquire. It is common place for seasoned chemical men to hide and hoard knowledge. They give fishes but don\u2019t teach how to fish. The only reason could be to be one up on the rest and wrest falthu respect.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nEver seen a derby race winner who as a colt was suppressed, disabled and crushed?</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPivZOF5UhI/AAAAAAAABSw/RWjvq75r2sQ/s1600/images+%252814%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPivZOF5UhI/AAAAAAAABSw/RWjvq75r2sQ/s1600/images+%252814%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nJunior ranks must be empowered to discover their potential and play the best game. The mentor must fill in the cracks of their vulnerabilities. The environment has to be punishment free and congenial. It must be such that a sailor can meet his needs while meeting the needs of the company.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTopnotch standards of performance need to be developed both personally and professionally.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nPerformance failure must be viewed as a gap between what is needed and what id produced. The OBM must describe and measure this gap. A mutual plan needs to be developed for closing the gap.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nEncourage employees to challenge the status quo. The OBM must convey companies standards and procedures.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nMentoring is also cost effective training for training can be done when time permits. Remember that ship runs round the clock. Audio visual aids are not required for training will be on the spot and hands on.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nAt the end of a successful mentoring programme it will be in order for a certificate of recognition to be issued to the mentee.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nThe image of the company should be such that employees want to remain with and outsiders want to be hired to.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nInvolve employees into decisions and discussions about budgeting.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nLack of competence tears down the infrastructure.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPivnwqSuRI/AAAAAAAABS0/WUUMr_f0lNU/s1600/images+%252815%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPivnwqSuRI/AAAAAAAABS0/WUUMr_f0lNU/s1600/images+%252815%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nSINCE OLD STYLE TRADITIONAL LOYALTY IS DEAD THE OBM HAS TO STRENGTHEN THE EMOTIONAL CONNECTION BETWEEN SHIPSTAFF AND COMPANY.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nWHAT MY VISION OF MENTORING IS NOT\u2014</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nWhen I was in a government public sector company as a junior officer I noticed that anybody who made it had a mentor. People in power cultivated prot\u00e9g\u00e9s as pawns in a power struggle. They sponsored their prot\u00e9g\u00e9es advancement without regard to merit. They taught their prot\u00e9g\u00e9es tricks of the trade such as skills to sabotage their competitors rather than develop their own talents. Such a person cannot be called a mentor.&nbsp;</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nA MENTOR CANNOT PLAY THE POWER GAME. The core value is not to have an alliance rather it is solely to develop the mentee. It is not a personal chemistry between 2 people or a training course. It is a deep trusting personal relationship where a two way flow of respect and kindness happens. OBM is a fresh set of eyes which see things differently.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nA mentor must not inappropriately achieve a promotion for the mentee or advance the mentees cause with his friends.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nSO THEN WHAT IS THE MENTOR WE ARE TALKING ABOUT---</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nThe mentor is not expected to sponsor his prot\u00e9g\u00e9e leading to favouristism , career climbing and internal politics. The playing field cannot be tilted by a true mentor in favour of the mentee. It is a one to one ,caring and helping relationship where the mentees professional growth is enhanced to prepare him for top notch performance and it rises above the mundane. If the mentee does not change for the better the mentoring exercise has not taken off.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiwA5ysEOI/AAAAAAAABS4/nQE4Iv2cnZg/s1600/images+%252816%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiwA5ysEOI/AAAAAAAABS4/nQE4Iv2cnZg/s1600/images+%252816%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIn the classic HOMER\u2019S ODYSSEY when Odysseus \u2013king of Ithaca leaves to fight in the Trojan war he entrusts the care of his household to MENTOR (easy name eh?, it could have been Balasubramaniamsivaramakrishnan \u2013tee hee!! In which case the title would have been OBB) who was the teacher of his son Telemachus.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIn time the word mentor has become synonymous with trusted friend,advisor ,teacher and sage. Examples of mentors and mentee in history are that of Socrates and Plato, Freud and Jung. Fagin of Oliver Twist who took homeless children under his wing to pick pockets for his own financial gain is not a mentor.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nA modern living legend who is a stern taskmaster can mould his prot\u00e9g\u00e9e to be a winner. The crunch word is \u2018care\u2019. A mentor cares for the mentee. Mentor\u2019s (of odyssey fame) job was not just to raise Telemachus, but to but to develop him for the responsibilities of a lifetime by touching every facet of his being. It goes beyond counseling or obligatory relationships.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIntuition , feelings , hunches \u2013all come to play in this intense long term relationship. The mentor gives a chance to the mentee to vent his negative feelings and get therapeutic relief.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nYou will appreciate in a ordinary training programme getting things off your chest may cause you to be black balled or worse cause the trainer to go into a deep sulk.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nSo what is the difference between a incompetent overbearing constantly nagging captain and a true mentor. They are on opposite ends of the pole ( tee hee!!).</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiwi4QWCfI/AAAAAAAABS8/jM1ShQMUn2s/s1600/images+%252818%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiwi4QWCfI/AAAAAAAABS8/jM1ShQMUn2s/s1600/images+%252818%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nThe mentor fills up performance gaps with information not nagging criticism. An OBM is a catalyst of change and creates synergy in the work force by proactively leading people to draw on their innate creative energy.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDO\u2019S FOR A OBM:</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIdentify things that do not meet your company standards. See if things can be done in a better way.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nGive insight to company culture, appropriate attitudes and special relevant insider knowledge that is not written anywhere.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nFocus on career plans and open new vistas for the mentee</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nGo that extra mile in discovering needs and fulfilling only those needs.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nCounseling that stretch the mentee must include personal experienced gleaned and distilled from past quality experience. All coaching must be consistent with organizational needs and values.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDiscuss stress management techniques on chemical tankers.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nHone win win negotiating and trust building skills.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiwx6SJ4OI/AAAAAAAABTA/MfZvWevKR3I/s1600/images+%252819%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiwx6SJ4OI/AAAAAAAABTA/MfZvWevKR3I/s1600/images+%252819%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nStrengthen communicating skills, team building skills and skills to bring people to consensus.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIdentify personal negative habits and reduce them.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nBuild assertive skills ( not aggressive skills )and conflict resolution skills.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nShow how to manage time productively by multitasking.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nBuild on positive thinking and optimism.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nCreate an atmosphere of trust.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nEnsure the OBM programme is a loose structure and flexible to meet the mentees needs.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nFocus on positive results of a transaction and encourage constructive imagination.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nAllow mentee to unload their troubles to get emotional release.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nLook out for creative ideas to improve the system.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDiscuss values and priorities.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nCreate a focus for creative energy by setting short term goals.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nObserve employees while on the job.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nEstablish time frames for corrective action.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nRespond to complaints quickly. Your door must be always open .( this is not like holding a chair on top of your head when told to take a chair --Tee hee !!)</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nFocus on efforts and contributions rather than accomplishments.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nEliminate barriers which prevent employees from unleashing their talents.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDON\u2019T\u2019S FOR THE OBM:</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t argue. Usually people argue without listening. They will only listen to gather information to reinforce their own arguments.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t expect instant change. Quick changes can be stressful and overwhelming. Remember you are there as an OBM to build a quality culture brick by brick.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t lower the mentees self esteem by threatening him to adopt new ways.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nThere is no need to push a reluctant soul too hard.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t take over a problem unless there is an imminent safety , pollution,</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\ncompany image crisis. Rescuing a mentee from mundane matters is not likely to help him in the long run.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t make any promises you cant keep. Don\u2019t over promise and underdeliver.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t encourage bickering or bitching.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiw_qrqSmI/AAAAAAAABTE/26m3jtGloxw/s1600/download.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiw_qrqSmI/AAAAAAAABTE/26m3jtGloxw/s1600/download.JPG\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t show favouritism. It can tear apart the work force.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t give negative feedback at the wrong time. Wrong time is not the time for a 2 way conversation.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t hold sessions disrespecting peoples time.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t win battles at the expense of losing the war.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t allow a insulting berating culture on board.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t compliment Dilton for his muscles and Big Moose for his brains (duh!).</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPixSKggxHI/AAAAAAAABTI/QoG-fWp-qo0/s1600/images+%252820%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPixSKggxHI/AAAAAAAABTI/QoG-fWp-qo0/s1600/images+%252820%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPixbmX0MEI/AAAAAAAABTQ/dUuDhsWwVfg/s1600/images+%252821%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPixbmX0MEI/AAAAAAAABTQ/dUuDhsWwVfg/s1600/images+%252821%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t produce your clone even if you are god\u2019s gift to shipping and this planet..</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nRELATIONSHIP BETWEEN MENTOR AND MENTEE:</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nThe mentee must feel comfortable with the mentor. Only then he will be willing to trust and open up the doors of his mind to receive solutions.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nLike a psychiatrist\u2019s professional code, negative things volunteered by the mentee must strictly remain with the mentor. This is why the mentor must have character.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nOnce a relationship is set up it can be carried on by email or telephone.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nFor such a trusting relationship the key words are \u2013encourage, help, listen, fair, caring, friendly, tolerant.etc.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nShare thoughts and act spontaneously.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTreat the mentee as an individual. Call yourself I --not WE as many superintendents do from their first day in office to rub in the fact that he is now the almighty company and dispenser of your destiny.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIf you are a seasoned guy, make sure you reduce the awe factor by being friendly.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nThe mentee must feel that you derive pleasure by helping him succeed and you want only good things to happen to him.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIf the mentor does not have an emotional attachment to his team all his techniques and smartness is of zilch use.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nA mentor broadens the horizons of the mentee.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPixsMeYLSI/AAAAAAAABTU/x_B0CSdUF5w/s1600/images+%252822%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"148\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPixsMeYLSI/AAAAAAAABTU/x_B0CSdUF5w/s320/images+%252822%2529.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTIPS FOR ASPIRING OBMS:</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nGive right help at the right time.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nEnable the mentee to solve his own problems.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nYou must be a volunteer (make sure you get paid too ) to this job\u2014only then can you enjoy it. Before you volunteer ask yourself \u201d Am I a mature intelligent and qualified individual for this abstract job?\u201d.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nOn an abstract mission things left unsaid usually speak more than what is said. Your commitment must be 100%. Your antenna must be tuned for reception. You must have a willingness to pause and listen. Do you have a freely giving nature or is your nature such that you give only when you get \u2018fayada\u2019 out of it. Can you stretch yourself to make a positive difference in the life of others?</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nSince this process is genuine , do not hesitate to terminate a mentoring relationship any time without assigning reasons. Remember you are a commitment building manager.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nSpontaneous off the cuff interventions while on the spot provide memorable and lasting learning experience.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nFeel for yourself if the work place gives nourishment to the soul and there is quality of life .</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nYou must do constant self improvement. Spent forces and deadwood will not get a calling card with QM printed on it.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nYou must know the ropes of body language. Only then you can forecast that something is amiss.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPix4hoSn6I/AAAAAAAABTY/NOymV4u77uA/s1600/images+%252823%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPix4hoSn6I/AAAAAAAABTY/NOymV4u77uA/s1600/images+%252823%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nBe aware that cultural differences complicate your task. Remember the coaching is OJT ( read that as on the job training )</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nWhen you get off the ship you must have done at least one thing to improve the happiness of crew on board. Even a simple thing like you were instrumental in getting a tt table or bad airconditioning repaired or procuring ergonomically friendly mattresses.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nMENTAL SHACKLES</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nPeople resist change only if they see no gain from it. They see only inconvenience and more inconvenience. Mentoring cannot be forced. It is like magic\u2014something like a religious conversion. ( not the type Dharmendra had to marry Hema Malini\u2014tee hee!!)</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nALSO ON THE UNSEEN AGENDA</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nSeek out individuals who are versatile, adaptable ( even to unfamiliar cultures ) and quick minded. Who are the guys who caught on right away?. Who are the marathon men? People who have energy ,vitality and enthusiasm pursue goals passionately. Energy included physical endurance and mental vigor.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiyJEIfDSI/AAAAAAAABTc/MkvTFlf3Eqk/s1600/images+%252824%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiyJEIfDSI/AAAAAAAABTc/MkvTFlf3Eqk/s1600/images+%252824%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTap the talent of excelsior guys.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nMaximize the strengths of the company and minimize the weaknesses.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nEvaluation is an integral part of the job. Even evaluating if it was a happy ship, whether the employees are upbeat, whether there is any discrimination.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nFor evaluating the officers\u2014key words are\u2014action oriented, approachable, patient, time manager, courage, endurance, innovation, integrity, vitality, vision, honesty, accountability, decisive, effective, ethical, setting priorities, multitasking , self starting etc.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nWho are the guys who walk on deck with a sense of purpose. A committed man rarely saunters around like a pregnant duck.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nCelebrations and parties on board are an extension of fun.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTRICKS:</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTo probe you need to ask open ended questions which cannot be answered with a terse yes or no. This is important to facilitate a meaningful discussion. A closed question terminates a conversation as soon as it is started . ( is beer a conversation opener? )</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nVirtually everyone has an emotional reaction (positive or negative )to certain trigger words. \u2018psychological deaf spots\u2019 often trigger an emotion reaction. ( better stick to the beer to open up the door of the mind --eh?)</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nFind common ground.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nView the whole crew as the orchestra band with the master as the conductor. Is the music pleasant to the ears. Whose guitar has to be restringed or violen tuned? Who are the pretenders who are screwing up the divine melody and giving music a bad name..</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nThe capacity to detect emotions and feelings and to respond appropriately ia a critical art of mentoring. Since feelings motivate people to do or undo things overlooking them or insensitiveness can severely limit the mentors effectiveness.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nRespect independence. Offer not push. Stick to helping not interfering.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nPractice the art of inclusion to build a stronger team.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nUnderstand that hierarchy is not simply a matter of rank or placing people on an organizational ladder. There are more profound and powerful hierarchies of competence, knowledge, seniority, talent, strength, intelligence, experience, influence , abstractions (ethics , loyalty , honor ,respect etc )etc.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t attempt to wish away this truth and learn things the hard way..</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nEven unpopular decisions are more easily accepted it they make good sense.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nMaintain your sense of humor. Fun activity should never be to embarrass .</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiyVDLqgTI/AAAAAAAABTg/m92NSquEMAI/s1600/images+%252825%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiyVDLqgTI/AAAAAAAABTg/m92NSquEMAI/s1600/images+%252825%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDon\u2019t give quick fix decisions. Rather thank the guy for bringing it to the company\u2019s notice.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nSupport and enable rather than restrict and oversee.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nAsk questions to understand \u2013not to challenge. Since you are not in the chain of command you can ask not tell.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDifferent people have different styles. Be sensitive to such differences.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nCommunicate, be patient, be passionate about the success of every mentee.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nUnderstand what is the meaning of win win solutions.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nListen for absolutes like never , every time etc.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nMISFIT OBM:</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nThe master is usually a misfit for OBM for when the going gets rough he is more interested in saving his own backside than the mentee\u2019s. Remember mentoring is an informal relationship outside the chain of command. Rank blinds us to the more subtle relationship required for mentoring. Also anxiety about performance evaluation stunts.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nCHEMICAL ENVIRONMENT:</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nHere the crew does more with less under stifling conditions.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nMany struggle with a feeling of overload. If they are uncertain about their futures crew will keep a low profile and constantly look over their shoulders.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nBurnouts are common place. Micromanaging is undesirable on chemical tankers unless the crew are all green horns and pretenders.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nSeagull managing is also not desirable\u2014fly in, bitch at all quack quack, crap of every body\u2019s heads and fly out.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiyitoOHbI/AAAAAAAABTk/O8uTJ-lAGhc/s1600/images+%252826%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"153\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPiyitoOHbI/AAAAAAAABTk/O8uTJ-lAGhc/s320/images+%252826%2529.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTHERE IS A REAL NEED FOR OBM ON CHEMICAL TANKERS WHERE CREW ARE CREATING THEIR OWN CAREER PATHS AND USING JOB HOPPING AS A SURE ROUTE TO PROFESSIONAL SUCCESS..</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nBOTTOM LINE:</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nA teacher says \u201c see you later\u201d</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nA OBM says \u201c keep in touch \u201c</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px;
