margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIntuition helps you stay in the present, like what is advocated in the Bhagavat Gita.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIt has little to do with predicting the future. . Playfulness and relaxation usually stimulate the intuitive process. All the human senses are channels for intuition and every cell can be an antenna to receive information</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIntuition is a gift of crisis--- It tells you the right thing to do when you don't have time to figure it all out.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIntuits are able to see possibilities and alternatives that aren\u2019t immediately apparent. Your inner knowing comes from first your instincts, second your intellect, and third from your intuition.<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPev82BdqbI/AAAAAAAABPE/52HMPygG_mY/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPev82BdqbI/AAAAAAAABPE/52HMPygG_mY/s640/images.jpg\" width=\"478\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIntuition is not pseudo-science . It is an essential psychological function like thinking, feeling and sensing. The divining power of intuition comes from our inner self. It arises from very rapid processing of bits of information that are stored in our subconscious. Intuition thinks in terms of metaphor, feelings, pictures, and the spatial whole and doesn't fit neatly into the cause-and-effect model.<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPewA25lBeI/AAAAAAAABPI/De9EhqFeaTs/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPewA25lBeI/AAAAAAAABPI/De9EhqFeaTs/s320/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" width=\"284\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIt is about trusting your own integrity - trusting your gut, trusting your heart.. . Your intuition will not force you to do things that are truly wrong for yourself or other people in contradiction with the laws of the universe. Intuition is listening to the inner voice or heeding the promptings from within.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIntuition is a ability to cut through the thickness of surface reality . Intuition and confidence go hand in hand. Your sub-conscious which operates a dozen times faster than your conscious mind has picked up on signals that your conscious mind has not yet processed. We function through partial information, and intuition gives us an overview, a whole sense of things. Intuition acts like a bridge between your logical reasoning and the sum total of your experience-based knowledge.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIntuition is a knowing, a sensing that is beyond the conscious understanding \u2014 a gut feeling-- flashes of spontaneous thought that are done apparently without relating to facts or logic. Intuition is fast, based on pattern matching.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPewUDf-PbI/AAAAAAAABPM/4gJI9pAzDwI/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"339\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPewUDf-PbI/AAAAAAAABPM/4gJI9pAzDwI/s400/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nThe divining power of intuition comes from our inner self-- very rapid processing of bits of information that are stored in our subconscious. We cannot command our gut feeling to use it at will. It just surfaces spontaneously when certain circumstances are present. Intuitive insights suddenly appear as ideas or feelings.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIntuition is now an EQ competency. It\u2019s considered something necessary to successful living, and something to be respected and valued. Intuitive decisions are NOT guesswork . Intuition has an important role to play in decision making . Intuition is not limited to opinions but can encompass the ability to know valid solutions to problems.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nIntuition usually shows up in the areas where you have passion and talent. By logic that we prove, by intuition we discover. Intuition is a sudden and inexplicable knowing. It lies at the roots of spontaneity, humor, creativity, inspiration, and even genius.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPeyP6tZrII/AAAAAAAABPg/9vnF1B_BnfQ/s1600/download.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPeyP6tZrII/AAAAAAAABPg/9vnF1B_BnfQ/s400/download.JPG\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br />\nIntuition has its own unique language for communicating with you through touch, sight, taste, sound, and smell. As you pay attention to your senses, you\u2019ll begin to understand the \u201cvocabulary\u201d of your intuition.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nMental static and ego can get in the way of tapping into intuition. Intuition bubbles up from within and can be overwhelmed by old mental or emotional \"tapes\" . Intuition gone wild becomes \u201cjumping to conclusions\u201d. By going too far out on a limb , you risk misinterpreting the situation and start harming others. Intuition should not be overused.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nYour brain is a complex tapestry of interacting neurons, all working together to provide you with insights that guide you through life. It\u2019s complicated. So complicated that your conscious brain cannot keep up with everything it\u2019s trying to tell you.<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPeyFK_cZgI/AAAAAAAABPY/ylW0DQxU7kg/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPeyFK_cZgI/AAAAAAAABPY/ylW0DQxU7kg/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nSo what exactly is intuition? It is the messages from your unconscious mind making contact with your consciousness. . The uncanny ability to detect patterns in the world around us, and to extrapolate larger truths . Use it always, never ignore it.<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPeyCHhkyAI/AAAAAAAABPU/PidezQJWxNg/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"567\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPeyCHhkyAI/AAAAAAAABPU/PidezQJWxNg/s640/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nOur instincts and intuition are more reliable in a decision making, than our conscious brain. . By listening to what our heart and soul tells us to do - and then doing it - we can take ourselves anywhere we have ever dreamed of going.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nYour consciousness only uses a tiny proportion of your brainpower and your intuition accesses the residual power and communicates to your consciousness the bank of wisdom and knowledge it has available. This is done subtly through thoughts, feelings, sensations, images, sounds or any combination of them. Just as animals have a natural survival instinct so humans are born with the natural ability to be intuitive; your human instinct.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nTraits often found in those with high intuitive intelligence include-- an awareness of one's personal value system, a healthy awareness of one's own feelings, an ability for self-direction and self-management, a powerful level of self-trust, a desire for innovation, a refined knowledge of one's strengths and weaknesses, and a high degree of self-regard and freedom.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n\"The only real valuable thing is intuition.\" -- Albert Einstein.</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nNever ignore the inner spark , the gut feeling, the sixth sense or hunch that ignites vision and leads you to success. Intuitive insights motivate us to grow closer to the creative source, thereby igniting our own creative spark and expression, which is the essence of our true self. When you feel excited about something, that's a hint about what to pursue.<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPexs8sll0I/AAAAAAAABPQ/DkCqvlMlH7E/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPexs8sll0I/AAAAAAAABPQ/DkCqvlMlH7E/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;\">Decisions are made in the mind\u2014choices are made in the gut.&nbsp;&nbsp;Choices come from your essence and attunement to your higher self.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;\"><i>Now -- having said all above, here is an amazing anatomy lesson. War victims have had their neural connection between spine and gut severed, still the bowel can function. This follows that the neural mass in the gut is an independent cognitive centre. This explains when as a Captain , I chew up a crew member &nbsp;for letting down the team, he gets severe intestinal gut cramps. And why anti-depressants targetting the brain solely, causes nausea. This means the brain and the gut are like Siamese twins. When one gets upset, the other one gets upset too. Half the nerve cells are situated in the gut. When i have a headache i target my gut by having an alkaseltzer, and it have never failed to work 100%. If your gut is unhealthy, your immunity lowers.</i></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;\"><i><br />\n</i></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-DOJeStVQV0Y/TWh1temXS7I/AAAAAAAADsk/BmgVBgHZvlk/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"292\" src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-DOJeStVQV0Y/TWh1temXS7I/AAAAAAAADsk/BmgVBgHZvlk/s320/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;\"><i><br />\n</i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 15px; line-height: 22px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\"><i>Both our gut and our brain originate early in embryo genesis from the same clump of tissue which divides during fetal development.&nbsp;</i></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/-od4aXr8lQyQ/TWh1qNMJo4I/AAAAAAAADsg/MGd06lGxJrQ/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"327\" src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/-od4aXr8lQyQ/TWh1qNMJo4I/AAAAAAAADsg/MGd06lGxJrQ/s400/images.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 15px; line-height: 22px;\"><i><br />\n</i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 22px;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 15px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\"></span>While one section turns into the central nervous system, another piece migrates to become the enteric nervous system. Later the two nervous systems connect via a cable called the </span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; color: red; font-size: large;\">vagus nerve</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 15px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\"> </span>\u2014 the longest of all the cranial nerves . The vagus nerve meanders from the brain stem through the neck and finally ends up in the abdomen. There\u2019s the brain-gut connection. This means your psychological health, is partly derived from the heathy gut. When you have severe dysentry , have you noticed how depressed you feel?</span></i></span><br />\n<div style=\"background: white; line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; vertical-align: top;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\nDevelop an intuitive life. This is not a tool-- it is a god given way of living.<br />\n<br />\nGrace and peace!<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://img.youtube.com/vi/J0vCnM0Gafg/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://youtube.googleapis.com/v/J0vCnM0Gafg&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://youtube.googleapis.com/v/J0vCnM0Gafg&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nCAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n..</div>\n</div>\n", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt.
